[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical security issue by the Jazzer fuzzing framework. This type of vulnerability[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability was discovered during a fuzzing session where:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressorGzipFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was configured to run with libfuzzer engine [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A total of [0m[1;36m551[0m[39m hooks from various security sanitizers were loaded, including OS [0m  [2m                [0m
